::: {#section-8 .section}
## [8.](#section-8){.section-number .selfRef} [UDP Periodic One-Way Delay and Loss Registry Entries](#name-udp-periodic-one-way-delay-){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-udp-periodic-one-way-delay-}

This section specifies five initial Registry Entries for UDP Periodic
One-Way Delay and one entry for UDP Periodic One-Way
Loss.[¶](#section-8-1){.pilcrow}

All column entries besides the ID, Name, Description, and Output
Reference Method categories are the same; thus, this section defines six
closely related Registry Entries. As a result, IANA has assigned
corresponding URLs to each of the six Named
Metrics.[¶](#section-8-2){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.1 .section}
### [8.1.](#section-8.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Summary](#name-summary-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-summary-5}

This category includes multiple indexes to the Registry Entries: the
element ID and Metric Name.[¶](#section-8.1-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.1.1 .section}
#### [8.1.1.](#section-8.1.1){.section-number .selfRef} [ID (Identifier)](#name-id-identifier-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-id-identifier-5}

IANA has allocated the numeric Identifiers 12-17 for the six Named
Metric Entries in [Section 8](#UDP_periodic_owd_and_loss){.xref}. See
[Section 8.1.2](#name812){.xref} for mapping to
Names.[¶](#section-8.1.1-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#name812}
::: {#section-8.1.2 .section}
#### [8.1.2.](#section-8.1.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Name](#name-name-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-name-5}

[]{.break}

12:
:   OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_95Percentile[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.2){.pilcrow}
:   

13:
:   OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Mean[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   

14:
:   OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Min[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.6){.pilcrow}
:   

15:
:   OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Max[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.8){.pilcrow}
:   

16:
:   OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_StdDev[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.10){.pilcrow}
:   

17:
:   OWLoss_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Percent_LossRatio[¶](#section-8.1.2-1.12){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.1.3 .section}
#### [8.1.3.](#section-8.1.3){.section-number .selfRef} [URI](#name-uri-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-uri-5}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_95Percentile>[¶](#section-8.1.3-1){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Mean>[¶](#section-8.1.3-2){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Min>[¶](#section-8.1.3-3){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_Max>[¶](#section-8.1.3-4){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWDelay_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Seconds_StdDev>[¶](#section-8.1.3-5){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/OWLoss_Active_IP-UDP-Periodic20m-Payload142B_RFC8912sec8_Percent_LossRatio>[¶](#section-8.1.3-6){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.1.4 .section}
#### [8.1.4.](#section-8.1.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Description](#name-description-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-description-5}

[]{.break}

OWDelay:

:   This metric assesses the delay of a stream of packets exchanged
    between two hosts (or measurement points) and reports the
    \<statistic> of one-way delay for all successfully exchanged packets
    based on their conditional delay
    distribution.[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.1){.pilcrow}

    where \<statistic> is one of:[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.2){.pilcrow}

    -   [95Percentile[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.1}
    -   [Mean[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.2){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.2}
    -   [Min[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.3){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.3}
    -   [Max[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.4){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.4}
    -   [StdDev[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.5){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.1.4-1.2.3.5}

:   

OWLoss:
:   This metric assesses the loss ratio of a stream of packets exchanged
    between two hosts (which are the two measurement points). The output
    is the one-way loss ratio for all transmitted packets expressed as a
    percentage.[¶](#section-8.1.4-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-8.1.5 .section}
#### [8.1.5.](#section-8.1.5){.section-number .selfRef} [Change Controller](#name-change-controller-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-change-controller-5}

IETF[¶](#section-8.1.5-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.1.6 .section}
#### [8.1.6.](#section-8.1.6){.section-number .selfRef} [Version (of Registry Format)](#name-version-of-registry-format-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-version-of-registry-format-5}

1.0[¶](#section-8.1.6-1){.pilcrow}
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.2 .section}
### [8.2.](#section-8.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Metric Definition](#name-metric-definition-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-metric-definition-5}

This category includes columns to prompt the entry of all necessary
details related to the metric definition, including the RFC reference
and values of input factors, called \"Fixed
Parameters\".[¶](#section-8.2-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.2.1 .section}
#### [8.2.1.](#section-8.2.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Definition](#name-reference-definition-9){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-definition-9}

For delay:[¶](#section-8.2.1-1){.pilcrow}

Almes, G., Kalidindi, S., Zekauskas, M., and A. Morton, Ed., \"A One-Way
Delay Metric for IP Performance Metrics (IPPM)\", STD 81, RFC 7679, DOI
10.17487/RFC7679, January 2016,
\<https://www.rfc-editor.org/info/rfc7679>.
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\][¶](#section-8.2.1-2){.pilcrow}

Morton, A. and E. Stephan, \"Spatial Composition of Metrics\", RFC 6049,
DOI 10.17487/RFC6049, January 2011,
\<https://www.rfc-editor.org/info/rfc6049>.
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\][¶](#section-8.2.1-3){.pilcrow}

[Section
3.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-3.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] provides the reference definition of the
singleton (single value) one-way delay metric. [Section
4.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-4.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] provides the reference definition
expanded to cover a multi-value sample. Note that terms such as
\"singleton\" and \"sample\" are defined in [Section
11](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-11){.relref} of
\[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.2.1-4){.pilcrow}

Only successful packet transfers with finite delay are included in the
sample, as prescribed in [Section
4.1.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.1.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.2.1-5){.pilcrow}

For loss:[¶](#section-8.2.1-6){.pilcrow}

Almes, G., Kalidindi, S., Zekauskas, M., and A. Morton, Ed., \"A One-Way
Loss Metric for IP Performance Metrics (IPPM)\", STD 82, RFC 7680, DOI
10.17487/RFC7680, January 2016,
\<https://www.rfc-editor.org/info/rfc7680>.
\[[RFC7680](#RFC7680){.xref}\][¶](#section-8.2.1-7){.pilcrow}

[Section
2.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7680#section-2.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC7680](#RFC7680){.xref}\] provides the reference definition of the
singleton (single value) one-way Loss metric. [Section
3.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7680#section-3.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC7680](#RFC7680){.xref}\] provides the reference definition
expanded to cover a multi-singleton sample. Note that terms such as
\"singleton\" and \"sample\" are defined in [Section
11](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-11){.relref} of
\[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.2.1-8){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.2.2 .section}
#### [8.2.2.](#section-8.2.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Fixed Parameters](#name-fixed-parameters-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-fixed-parameters-5}

[]{.break}

Type-P:
:   []{.break}

    IPv4 header values:
    :   []{.break}

        DSCP:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   

        TTL:
        :   Set to 255[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.4){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Protocol:
        :   Set to 17 (UDP)[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.6){.pilcrow}
        :   
    :   

    []{.break}

    IPv6 header values:
    :   []{.break}

        DSCP:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.3.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Hop Count:
        :   Set to 255[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.3.2.2.4){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Next Header:
        :   Set to 17 (UDP)[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.3.2.2.6){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Flow Label:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.3.2.2.8){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Extension Headers:
        :   None[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.3.2.2.10){.pilcrow}
        :   
    :   

    []{.break}

    UDP header values:
    :   []{.break}

        Checksum:
        :   The checksum [MUST]{.bcp14} be calculated and the non-zero
            checksum included in the
            header[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.4.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   
    :   

    []{.break}

    UDP Payload:

    :   TWAMP-Test packet formats ([Section
        4.1.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5357#section-4.1.2){.relref}
        of
        \[[RFC5357](#RFC5357){.xref}\])[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.5.2.1){.pilcrow}

        -   [Security features in use influence the number of Padding
            octets[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.5.2.2.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.2.2-1.2.5.2.2.1}
        -   [142 octets total, including the TWAMP format (and format
            type [MUST]{.bcp14} be reported, if
            used)[¶](#section-8.2.2-1.2.5.2.2.2){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.2.2-1.2.5.2.2.2}

    :   
:   

[]{.break}

Other measurement Parameters:
:   []{.break}

    Tmax:
    :   A loss threshold waiting time with value 3.0, expressed in units
        of seconds, as a positive value of type decimal64 with fraction
        digits = 4 (see [Section
        9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref}
        of \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) and with a resolution of
        0.0001 seconds (0.1 ms), with lossless conversion to/from the
        32-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
        6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
        \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.2.2-2.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
    :   
:   

See the Packet Stream Generation section for three additional Fixed
Parameters.[¶](#section-8.2.2-3){.pilcrow}
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.3 .section}
### [8.3.](#section-8.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Method of Measurement](#name-method-of-measurement-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-method-of-measurement-5}

This category includes columns for references to relevant sections of
the RFC(s) and any supplemental information needed to ensure an
unambiguous method for implementations.[¶](#section-8.3-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.3.1 .section}
#### [8.3.1.](#section-8.3.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Methods](#name-reference-methods-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-methods-5}

The methodology for this metric (equivalent to
Type-P-One-way-Delay-Poisson-Stream) is defined as in [Section
3.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-3.6){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] (for singletons) and [Section
4.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-4.6){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] (for samples) using the Type-P and Tmax
defined in the Fixed Parameters column. However, a Periodic stream is
used, as defined in
\[[RFC3432](#RFC3432){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.3.1-1){.pilcrow}

The reference method distinguishes between long-delayed packets and lost
packets by implementing a maximum waiting time for packet arrival. Tmax
is the waiting time used as the threshold to declare a packet lost. Lost
packets [SHALL]{.bcp14} be designated as having undefined delay and
counted for the OWLoss metric.[¶](#section-8.3.1-2){.pilcrow}

The calculations on the one-way delay [SHALL]{.bcp14} be performed on
the conditional distribution, conditioned on successful packet arrival
within Tmax. Also, when all packet delays are stored, the process that
calculates the one-way delay value [MUST]{.bcp14} enforce the Tmax
threshold on stored values before calculations. See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.3.1-3){.pilcrow}

The reference method requires some way to distinguish between different
packets in a stream to establish correspondence between sending times
and receiving times for each successfully arriving
packet.[¶](#section-8.3.1-4){.pilcrow}

Since a standard measurement protocol is employed
\[[RFC5357](#RFC5357){.xref}\], the measurement process will determine
the sequence numbers or timestamps applied to test packets after the
Fixed and Runtime Parameters are passed to that process. The measurement
protocol dictates the format of sequence numbers and timestamps conveyed
in the TWAMP-Test packet payload.[¶](#section-8.3.1-5){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.3.2 .section}
#### [8.3.2.](#section-8.3.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Packet Stream Generation](#name-packet-stream-generation-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-packet-stream-generation-5}

This section provides details regarding packet traffic, which is used as
the basis for measurement. In IPPM Metrics, this is called the
\"stream\"; this stream can easily be described by providing the list of
stream Parameters.[¶](#section-8.3.2-1){.pilcrow}

[Section 3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3432#section-3){.relref}
of \[[RFC3432](#RFC3432){.xref}\] prescribes the method for generating
Periodic streams using associated
Parameters.[¶](#section-8.3.2-2){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

incT:
:   The nominal duration of the inter-packet interval, first bit to
    first bit, with value 0.0200, expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 4 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) and with a resolution of 0.0001
    seconds (0.1 ms), with lossless conversion to/from the 32-bit NTP
    timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.3.2-3.2){.pilcrow}
:   

dT:
:   The duration of the interval for allowed sample start times, with
    value 1.0000, expressed in units of seconds, as a positive value of
    type decimal64 with fraction digits = 4 (see [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) and with a resolution of 0.0001
    seconds (0.1 ms), with lossless conversion to/from the 32-bit NTP
    timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.3.2-3.4){.pilcrow}
:   

T0:
:   The actual start time of the periodic stream, determined from T0 and
    dT.[¶](#section-8.3.2-3.6){.pilcrow}
:   

Note: An initiation process with a number of control exchanges resulting
in unpredictable start times (within a time interval) may be sufficient
to avoid synchronization of periodic streams and is a valid replacement
for selecting a start time at random from a fixed
interval.[¶](#section-8.3.2-4){.pilcrow}

These stream Parameters will be specified as Runtime
Parameters.[¶](#section-8.3.2-5){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.3.3 .section}
#### [8.3.3.](#section-8.3.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Traffic Filtering (Observation) Details](#name-traffic-filtering-observation-d){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-traffic-filtering-observation-d}

N/A[¶](#section-8.3.3-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.3.4 .section}
#### [8.3.4.](#section-8.3.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Sampling Distribution](#name-sampling-distribution-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-sampling-distribution-5}

N/A[¶](#section-8.3.4-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.3.5 .section}
#### [8.3.5.](#section-8.3.5){.section-number .selfRef} [Runtime Parameters and Data Format](#name-runtime-parameters-and-data-for){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-runtime-parameters-and-data-for}

Runtime Parameters are input factors that must be determined, configured
into the measurement system, and reported with the results for the
context to be complete.[¶](#section-8.3.5-1){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Src:
:   The IP address of the host in the Src Role (format
    ipv4‑address-no-zone value for IPv4 or ipv6-address-no-zone value
    for IPv6; see [Section
    4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-4){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]).[¶](#section-8.3.5-2.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Dst:
:   The IP address of the host in the Dst Role (format
    ipv4‑address-no-zone value for IPv4 or ipv6-address-no-zone value
    for IPv6; see [Section
    4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-4){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]).[¶](#section-8.3.5-2.4){.pilcrow}
:   

T0:
:   A time, the start of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as
    specified in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\]. When T0 is \"all-zeros\", a start
    time is unspecified and Tf is to be interpreted as the duration of
    the measurement interval. The start time is controlled through other
    means.[¶](#section-8.3.5-2.6){.pilcrow}
:   

Tf:
:   A time, the end of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as
    specified in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\]. When T0 is \"all-zeros\", an ending
    time and date is ignored and Tf is interpreted as the duration of
    the measurement interval.[¶](#section-8.3.5-2.8){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-8.3.6 .section}
#### [8.3.6.](#section-8.3.6){.section-number .selfRef} [Roles](#name-roles-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-roles-5}

[]{.break}

Src:
:   Launches each packet and waits for return transmissions from the
    Dst.  An example is the TWAMP
    Session-Sender.[¶](#section-8.3.6-1.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Dst:
:   Waits for each packet from the Src and sends a return packet to the
    Src.  An example is the TWAMP
    Session-Reflector.[¶](#section-8.3.6-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.4 .section}
### [8.4.](#section-8.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Output](#name-output-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-output-5}

This category specifies all details of the output of measurements using
the metric.[¶](#section-8.4-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.4.1 .section}
#### [8.4.1.](#section-8.4.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Type](#name-type-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-type-5}

Latency and Loss Types are discussed in the subsections
below.[¶](#section-8.4.1-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.4.2 .section}
#### [8.4.2.](#section-8.4.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Definition](#name-reference-definition-10){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-definition-10}

For all output types:[¶](#section-8.4.2-1){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

T0:
:   The start of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as
    specified in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2-2.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Tf:
:   The end of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as specified
    in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2-2.4){.pilcrow}
:   

For LossRatio, the count of lost packets to total packets sent is the
basis for the loss ratio calculation as per [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7680#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC7680](#RFC7680){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2-3){.pilcrow}

For each \<statistic> or Percent_LossRatio, one of the following
subsections applies.[¶](#section-8.4.2-4){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.4.2.1 .section}
##### [8.4.2.1.](#section-8.4.2.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Percentile95](#name-percentile95-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-percentile95-2}

The 95th percentile [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of one-way delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.1-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.4.2.1-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the percentile statistic
(where round-trip delay should be substituted for
\"ipdv\").[¶](#section-8.4.2.1-3){.pilcrow}

The percentile = 95, meaning that the reported delay, \"95Percentile\",
is the smallest value of one-way delay for which the Empirical
Distribution Function, EDF(95Percentile), is greater than or equal to
95% of the singleton one-way delay values in the conditional
distribution. See [Section
11.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-11.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\] for the definition of the percentile
statistic using the EDF.[¶](#section-8.4.2.1-4){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

95Percentile:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of 0.000000001
    seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from the 64-bit
    NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.1-5.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#mean-sec8422}
::: {#section-8.4.2.2 .section}
##### [8.4.2.2.](#section-8.4.2.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Mean](#name-mean-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-mean-2}

The mean [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of one-way delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.2-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.4.2.2-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.2.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.2.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for details on calculating this
statistic; see also [Section
4.2.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.2.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.2-3){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Mean:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.2-4.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.4.2.3 .section}
##### [8.4.2.3.](#section-8.4.2.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Min](#name-min-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-min-2}

The minimum [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of one-way delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.3-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.4.2.3-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.3.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for details on calculating this
statistic; see also [Section
4.3.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.3-3){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Min:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.3-4.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-8.4.2.4 .section}
##### [8.4.2.4.](#section-8.4.2.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Max](#name-max-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-max-2}

The maximum [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of one-way delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.3.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for a closely related method for
calculating this statistic; see also [Section
4.3.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\]. The formula is as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-3){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.4.2.4-4 .alignLeft .art-text .artwork}
       Max = (FiniteDelay[j])

[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-4){.pilcrow}
:::

-   [such that for some index, j, where 1 \<= j \<= N
    FiniteDelay\[j\] >= FiniteDelay\[n\] for all
    n[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-5.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.2.4-5.1}

[]{.break}

Max:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.4-6.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-8.4.2.5 .section}
##### [8.4.2.5.](#section-8.4.2.5){.section-number .selfRef} [Std_Dev](#name-std_dev-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-std_dev-2}

Std_Dev [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional distribution
of all packets with a finite value of one‑way delay (undefined delays
are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
6.1.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-6.1.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for a closely related method for
calculating this statistic. The formula is the classic calculation for
the standard deviation of a population.[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-3){.pilcrow}

Define Population Std_Dev_Delay as
follows:[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-4){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-8.4.2.5-5 .alignLeft .art-text .artwork}
                         _                                       _
                        |            N                            |
                        |           ---                           |
                        |     1     \                          2  |
        Std_Dev = SQRT  |  -------   >   (Delay[n] - MeanDelay)   |
                        |    (N)    /                             |
                        |           ---                           |
                        |          n = 1                          |
                        |_                                       _|

[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-5){.pilcrow}
:::

where all packets n = 1 through N have a value for Delay\[n\], MeanDelay
is calculated per [Section 8.4.2.2](#mean-sec8422){.xref}, and SQRT\[\]
is the Square Root function:[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-6){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Std_Dev:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of 0.000000001
    seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from the 64-bit
    NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.2.5-7.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-8.4.2.6 .section}
##### [8.4.2.6.](#section-8.4.2.6){.section-number .selfRef} [Percent_LossRatio](#name-percent_lossratio-2){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-percent_lossratio-2}

[]{.break}

Percent_LossRatio:
:   The numeric value of the result is expressed in units of lost
    packets to total packets times 100%, as a positive value of type
    decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\] with a resolution of
    0.0000000001.[¶](#section-8.4.2.6-1.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.4.3 .section}
#### [8.4.3.](#section-8.4.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Metric Units](#name-metric-units-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-metric-units-5}

The \<statistic> of one-way delay is expressed in seconds, where
\<statistic> is one of:[¶](#section-8.4.3-1){.pilcrow}

-   [95Percentile[¶](#section-8.4.3-2.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.3-2.1}
-   [Mean[¶](#section-8.4.3-2.2){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.3-2.2}
-   [Min[¶](#section-8.4.3-2.3){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.3-2.3}
-   [Max[¶](#section-8.4.3-2.4){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.3-2.4}
-   [StdDev[¶](#section-8.4.3-2.5){.pilcrow}]{#section-8.4.3-2.5}

The one-way loss ratio is expressed as a percentage of lost packets to
total packets sent.[¶](#section-8.4.3-3){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-8.4.4 .section}
#### [8.4.4.](#section-8.4.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Calibration](#name-calibration-5){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-calibration-5}

[Section
3.7.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-3.7.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] provides a means to quantify the
systematic and random errors of a time measurement. Calibration in-situ
could be enabled with an internal loopback that includes as much of the
measurement system as possible, performs address manipulation as needed,
and provides some form of isolation (e.g., deterministic delay) to avoid
send-receive interface contention. Some portion of the random and
systematic error can be characterized in this
way.[¶](#section-8.4.4-1){.pilcrow}

For one-way delay measurements, the error calibration must include an
assessment of the internal clock synchronization with its external
reference (this internal clock is supplying timestamps for measurement).
In practice, the time offsets \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\] of clocks
at both the Source and Destination are needed to estimate the systematic
error due to imperfect clock synchronization (the time offsets
\[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\] are smoothed; thus, the random variation
is not usually represented in the
results).[¶](#section-8.4.4-2){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

time_offset:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    signed value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of 0.000000001
    seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from the 64-bit
    NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-8.4.4-3.2){.pilcrow}
:   

When a measurement controller requests a calibration measurement, the
loopback is applied and the result is output in the same format as a
normal measurement, with an additional indication that it is a
calibration result. In any measurement, the measurement function
[SHOULD]{.bcp14} report its current estimate of the time offset
\[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\] as an indicator of the degree of
synchronization.[¶](#section-8.4.4-4){.pilcrow}

Both internal loopback calibration and clock synchronization can be used
to estimate the available accuracy of the Output Metric Units. For
example, repeated loopback delay measurements will reveal the portion of
the output result resolution that is the result of system noise and is
thus inaccurate.[¶](#section-8.4.4-5){.pilcrow}
:::
:::

::: {#section-8.5 .section}

Current[¶](#section-8.5.1-1){.pilcrow}

:::

1.0[¶](#section-8.5.3-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9 .section}
## [9.](#section-9){.section-number .selfRef} [ICMP Round-Trip Latency and Loss Registry Entries](#name-icmp-round-trip-latency-and){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-icmp-round-trip-latency-and}

This section specifies three initial Registry Entries for ICMP
Round‑Trip Latency and another entry for the ICMP Round-Trip Loss
Ratio.[¶](#section-9-1){.pilcrow}

All column entries besides the ID, Name, Description, and Output
Reference Method categories are the same; thus, this section defines
four closely related Registry Entries. As a result, IANA has assigned
corresponding URLs to each of the four Named
Metrics.[¶](#section-9-2){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.1 .section}
### [9.1.](#section-9.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Summary](#name-summary-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-summary-6}

This category includes multiple indexes to the Registry Entries: the
element ID and Metric Name.[¶](#section-9.1-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.1.1 .section}
#### [9.1.1.](#section-9.1.1){.section-number .selfRef} [ID (Identifier)](#name-id-identifier-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-id-identifier-6}

IANA has allocated the numeric Identifiers 18-21 for the four Named
Metric Entries in [Section 9](#icmp_roundtrip_latency_and_loss){.xref}.
See [Section 9.1.2](#name912){.xref} for mapping to
Names.[¶](#section-9.1.1-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#name912}
::: {#section-9.1.2 .section}
#### [9.1.2.](#section-9.1.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Name](#name-name-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-name-6}

[]{.break}

18:
:   RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Mean[¶](#section-9.1.2-1.2){.pilcrow}
:   

19:
:   RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Min[¶](#section-9.1.2-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   

20:
:   RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Max[¶](#section-9.1.2-1.6){.pilcrow}
:   

21:
:   RTLoss_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Percent_LossRatio[¶](#section-9.1.2-1.8){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-9.1.3 .section}
#### [9.1.3.](#section-9.1.3){.section-number .selfRef} [URI](#name-uri-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-uri-6}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Mean>[¶](#section-9.1.3-1){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Min>[¶](#section-9.1.3-2){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/RTDelay_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Seconds_Max>[¶](#section-9.1.3-3){.pilcrow}

URL:
<https://www.iana.org/assignments/performance-metrics/RTLoss_Active_IP-ICMP-SendOnRcv_RFC8912sec9_Percent_LossRatio>[¶](#section-9.1.3-4){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.1.4 .section}
#### [9.1.4.](#section-9.1.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Description](#name-description-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-description-6}

[]{.break}

RTDelay:

:   This metric assesses the delay of a stream of ICMP packets exchanged
    between two hosts (which are the two measurement points). The output
    is the round-trip delay for all successfully exchanged packets
    expressed as the \<statistic> of their conditional delay
    distribution, where \<statistic> is one
    of:[¶](#section-9.1.4-1.2.1){.pilcrow}

    -   [Mean[¶](#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.1}
    -   [Min[¶](#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.2){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.2}
    -   [Max[¶](#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.3){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.1.4-1.2.2.3}

:   

RTLoss:
:   This metric assesses the loss ratio of a stream of ICMP packets
    exchanged between two hosts (which are the two measurement points).
    The output is the round-trip loss ratio for all transmitted packets
    expressed as a percentage.[¶](#section-9.1.4-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-9.1.5 .section}
#### [9.1.5.](#section-9.1.5){.section-number .selfRef} [Change Controller](#name-change-controller-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-change-controller-6}

IETF[¶](#section-9.1.5-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.1.6 .section}
#### [9.1.6.](#section-9.1.6){.section-number .selfRef} [Version (of Registry Format)](#name-version-of-registry-format-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-version-of-registry-format-6}

1.0[¶](#section-9.1.6-1){.pilcrow}
:::
:::

::: {#section-9.2 .section}
### [9.2.](#section-9.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Metric Definition](#name-metric-definition-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-metric-definition-6}

This category includes columns to prompt the entry of all necessary
details related to the metric definition, including the RFC reference
and values of input factors, called \"Fixed
Parameters\".[¶](#section-9.2-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.2.1 .section}
#### [9.2.1.](#section-9.2.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Definition](#name-reference-definition-11){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-definition-11}

For delay:[¶](#section-9.2.1-1){.pilcrow}

Almes, G., Kalidindi, S., and M. Zekauskas, \"A Round-trip Delay Metric
for IPPM\", RFC 2681, DOI 10.17487/RFC2681, September 1999,
\<https://www.rfc-editor.org/info/rfc2681>.
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\][¶](#section-9.2.1-2){.pilcrow}

[Section
2.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-2.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] provides the reference definition of the
singleton (single value) round-trip delay metric. [Section
3.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-3.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] provides the reference definition
expanded to cover a multi-singleton sample. Note that terms such as
\"singleton\" and \"sample\" are defined in [Section
11](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-11){.relref} of
\[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.2.1-3){.pilcrow}

Note that although the definition of round-trip delay between the Source
(Src) and the Destination (Dst) as provided in [Section
2.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-2.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] is directionally ambiguous in the text,
this metric tightens the definition further to recognize that the host
in the Src Role will send the first packet to the host in the Dst Role
and will ultimately receive the corresponding return packet from the Dst
(when neither is lost).[¶](#section-9.2.1-4){.pilcrow}

Finally, note that the variable \"dT\" is used in
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] to refer to the value of round-trip delay
in metric definitions and methods. The variable \"dT\" has been reused
in other IPPM literature to refer to different quantities and cannot be
used as a global variable name.[¶](#section-9.2.1-5){.pilcrow}

For loss:[¶](#section-9.2.1-6){.pilcrow}

Morton, A., \"Round-Trip Packet Loss Metrics\", RFC 6673, DOI
10.17487/RFC6673, August 2012,
\<https://www.rfc-editor.org/info/rfc6673>.
\[[RFC6673](#RFC6673){.xref}\][¶](#section-9.2.1-7){.pilcrow}

Both Delay and Loss metrics employ a maximum waiting time for received
packets, so the count of lost packets to total packets sent is the basis
for the loss ratio calculation as per [Section
6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6673#section-6.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC6673](#RFC6673){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.2.1-8){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.2.2 .section}
#### [9.2.2.](#section-9.2.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Fixed Parameters](#name-fixed-parameters-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-fixed-parameters-6}

[]{.break}

Type-P as defined in [Section 13](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-13){.relref} of \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\]:
:   []{.break}

    IPv4 header values:
    :   []{.break}

        DSCP:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   

        TTL:
        :   Set to 255[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.4){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Protocol:
        :   Set to 01 (ICMP)[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.2.2.6){.pilcrow}
        :   
    :   

    IPv6 header values:
    :   []{.break}

        DSCP:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.4.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Hop Count:
        :   Set to 255[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.4.2.4){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Next Header:
        :   Set to 128 decimal
            (ICMP)[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.4.2.6){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Flow Label:
        :   Set to 0[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.4.2.8){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Extension Headers:
        :   None[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.4.2.10){.pilcrow}
        :   
    :   

    ICMP header values:
    :   []{.break}

        Type:
        :   8 (Echo Request)[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.6.2.2){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Code:
        :   0[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.6.2.4){.pilcrow}
        :   

        Checksum:
        :   The checksum [MUST]{.bcp14} be calculated and the non-zero
            checksum included in the
            header[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.6.2.6){.pilcrow}
        :   

        (Identifier and sequence number set at runtime)

        :   

        :   
    :   

    ICMP Payload:
    :   Total of 32 bytes of random information, constant per
        test[¶](#section-9.2.2-1.2.2.8){.pilcrow}
    :   
:   

[]{.break}

Other measurement Parameters:
:   []{.break}

    Tmax:
    :   A loss threshold waiting time with value 3.0, expressed in units
        of seconds, as a positive value of type decimal64 with fraction
        digits = 4 (see [Section
        9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref}
        of \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) and with a resolution of
        0.0001 seconds (0.1 ms), with lossless conversion to/from the
        32-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
        6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
        \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.2.2-2.2.2.2){.pilcrow}
    :   
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-9.3 .section}
### [9.3.](#section-9.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Method of Measurement](#name-method-of-measurement-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-method-of-measurement-6}

This category includes columns for references to relevant sections of
the RFC(s) and any supplemental information needed to ensure an
unambiguous method for implementations.[¶](#section-9.3-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.3.1 .section}
#### [9.3.1.](#section-9.3.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Methods](#name-reference-methods-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-methods-6}

The methodology for this metric (equivalent to
Type-P-Round-trip-Delay-Poisson-Stream) is defined as in [Section
2.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-2.6){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] (for singletons) and [Section
3.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-3.6){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\] (for samples) using the Type-P and Tmax
defined in the Fixed Parameters column.[¶](#section-9.3.1-1){.pilcrow}

The reference method distinguishes between long-delayed packets and lost
packets by implementing a maximum waiting time for packet arrival. Tmax
is the waiting time used as the threshold to declare a packet lost. Lost
packets [SHALL]{.bcp14} be designated as having undefined delay and
counted for the RTLoss metric.[¶](#section-9.3.1-2){.pilcrow}

The calculations on the delay (RTD) [SHALL]{.bcp14} be performed on the
conditional distribution, conditioned on successful packet arrival
within Tmax. Also, when all packet delays are stored, the process that
calculates the RTD value [MUST]{.bcp14} enforce the Tmax threshold on
stored values before calculations. See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-9.3.1-3){.pilcrow}

The reference method requires some way to distinguish between different
packets in a stream to establish correspondence between sending times
and receiving times for each successfully arriving packet. Sequence
numbers or other send-order identification [MUST]{.bcp14} be retained at
the Src or included with each packet to disambiguate packet reordering
if it occurs.[¶](#section-9.3.1-4){.pilcrow}

The measurement process will determine the sequence numbers applied to
test packets after the Fixed and Runtime Parameters are passed to that
process. The ICMP measurement process and protocol will dictate the
format of sequence numbers and other
Identifiers.[¶](#section-9.3.1-5){.pilcrow}

Refer to [Section
4.4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6673#section-4.4){.relref} of
\[[RFC6673](#RFC6673){.xref}\] for an expanded discussion of the
instruction to \"send a Type-P packet back to the Src as quickly as
possible\" in [Section
2.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2681#section-2.6){.relref} of
\[[RFC2681](#RFC2681){.xref}\]. [Section
8](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6673#section-8){.relref} of
\[[RFC6673](#RFC6673){.xref}\] presents additional requirements that
[MUST]{.bcp14} be included in the Method of Measurement for this
metric.[¶](#section-9.3.1-6){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.3.2 .section}
#### [9.3.2.](#section-9.3.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Packet Stream Generation](#name-packet-stream-generation-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-packet-stream-generation-6}

This section provides details regarding packet traffic, which is used as
the basis for measurement. In IPPM Metrics, this is called the
\"stream\"; this stream can easily be described by providing the list of
stream Parameters.[¶](#section-9.3.2-1){.pilcrow}

The ICMP metrics use a sending discipline called \"SendOnRcv\" or Send
On Receive. This is a modification of [Section
3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3432#section-3){.relref} of
\[[RFC3432](#RFC3432){.xref}\], which prescribes the method for
generating Periodic streams using associated Parameters as defined below
for this description:[¶](#section-9.3.2-2){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

incT:
:   The nominal duration of the inter-packet interval, first bit to
    first bit.[¶](#section-9.3.2-3.2){.pilcrow}
:   

dT:
:   The duration of the interval for allowed sample start
    times.[¶](#section-9.3.2-3.4){.pilcrow}
:   

The incT stream Parameter will be specified as a Runtime Parameter, and
dT is not used in SendOnRcv.[¶](#section-9.3.2-4){.pilcrow}

A SendOnRcv sender behaves exactly like a Periodic stream generator
while all reply packets arrive with RTD \< incT, and the inter-packet
interval will be constant.[¶](#section-9.3.2-5){.pilcrow}

If a reply packet arrives with RTD \>= incT, then the inter-packet
interval for the next sending time is nominally
RTD.[¶](#section-9.3.2-6){.pilcrow}

If a reply packet fails to arrive within Tmax, then the inter-packet
interval for the next sending time is nominally
Tmax.[¶](#section-9.3.2-7){.pilcrow}

If an immediate Send On Reply arrival is desired, then set
incT = 0.[¶](#section-9.3.2-8){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.3.3 .section}
#### [9.3.3.](#section-9.3.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Traffic Filtering (Observation) Details](#name-traffic-filtering-observation-de){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-traffic-filtering-observation-de}

N/A[¶](#section-9.3.3-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.3.4 .section}
#### [9.3.4.](#section-9.3.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Sampling Distribution](#name-sampling-distribution-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-sampling-distribution-6}

N/A[¶](#section-9.3.4-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.3.5 .section}
#### [9.3.5.](#section-9.3.5){.section-number .selfRef} [Runtime Parameters and Data Format](#name-runtime-parameters-and-data-form){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-runtime-parameters-and-data-form}

Runtime Parameters are input factors that must be determined, configured
into the measurement system, and reported with the results for the
context to be complete.[¶](#section-9.3.5-1){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Src:
:   The IP address of the host in the Src Role (format
    ipv4‑address-no-zone value for IPv4 or ipv6-address-no-zone value
    for IPv6; see [Section
    4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-4){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]).[¶](#section-9.3.5-2.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Dst:
:   The IP address of the host in the Dst Role (format
    ipv4‑address-no-zone value for IPv4 or ipv6-address-no-zone value
    for IPv6; see [Section
    4](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-4){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]).[¶](#section-9.3.5-2.4){.pilcrow}
:   

incT:
:   The nominal duration of the inter-packet interval, first bit to
    first bit, expressed in units of seconds, as a positive value of
    type decimal64 with fraction digits = 4 (see [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) and with a resolution of 0.0001
    seconds (0.1 ms).[¶](#section-9.3.5-2.6){.pilcrow}
:   

T0:
:   A time, the start of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as
    specified in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\]. When T0 is \"all-zeros\", a start
    time is unspecified and Tf is to be interpreted as the duration of
    the measurement interval. The start time is controlled through other
    means.[¶](#section-9.3.5-2.8){.pilcrow}
:   

Count:
:   The total count of ICMP Echo Requests to send, formatted as a
    uint16, as per [Section
    9.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.2){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.3.5-2.10){.pilcrow}
:   

See the Packet Stream Generation section for additional Runtime
Parameters.[¶](#section-9.3.5-3){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.3.6 .section}
#### [9.3.6.](#section-9.3.6){.section-number .selfRef} [Roles](#name-roles-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-roles-6}

[]{.break}

Src:
:   Launches each packet and waits for return transmissions from the
    Dst.[¶](#section-9.3.6-1.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Dst:
:   Waits for each packet from the Src and sends a return packet to the
    Src (ICMP Echo Reply, Type 0).[¶](#section-9.3.6-1.4){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-9.4 .section}
### [9.4.](#section-9.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Output](#name-output-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-output-6}

This category specifies all details of the output of measurements using
the metric.[¶](#section-9.4-1){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.4.1 .section}
#### [9.4.1.](#section-9.4.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Type](#name-type-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-type-6}

Latency and Loss Types are discussed in the subsections
below.[¶](#section-9.4.1-1){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.4.2 .section}
#### [9.4.2.](#section-9.4.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Reference Definition](#name-reference-definition-12){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-reference-definition-12}

For all output types:[¶](#section-9.4.2-1){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

T0:
:   The start of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as
    specified in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2-2.2){.pilcrow}
:   

Tf:
:   The end of a measurement interval (format \"date‑time\" as specified
    in [Section
    5.6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339#section-5.6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC3339](#RFC3339){.xref}\]; see also \"date‑and‑time\" in
    [Section
    3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6991#section-3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6991](#RFC6991){.xref}\]). The UTC Time Zone is required by
    [Section
    6.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2330#section-6.1){.relref} of
    \[[RFC2330](#RFC2330){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2-2.4){.pilcrow}
:   

TotalCount:
:   The count of packets actually sent by the Src to the Dst during the
    measurement interval.[¶](#section-9.4.2-2.6){.pilcrow}
:   

For each \<statistic> or Percent_LossRatio, one of the following
subsections applies.[¶](#section-9.4.2-3){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.4.2.1 .section}
##### [9.4.2.1.](#section-9.4.2.1){.section-number .selfRef} [Mean](#name-mean-3){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-mean-3}

The mean [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of round-trip delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-9.4.2.1-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-9.4.2.1-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.2.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.2.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for details on calculating this
statistic; see also [Section
4.2.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.2.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.1-3){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Mean:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.1-4.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-9.4.2.2 .section}
##### [9.4.2.2.](#section-9.4.2.2){.section-number .selfRef} [Min](#name-min-3){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-min-3}

The minimum [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of round-trip delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-9.4.2.2-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-9.4.2.2-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.3.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for details on calculating this
statistic; see also [Section
4.3.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.2-3){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Min:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.2-4.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-9.4.2.3 .section}
##### [9.4.2.3.](#section-9.4.2.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Max](#name-max-3){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-max-3}

The maximum [SHALL]{.bcp14} be calculated using the conditional
distribution of all packets with a finite value of round-trip delay
(undefined delays are excluded) \-- a single value, as
follows:[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-1){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3393#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC3393](#RFC3393){.xref}\] for details on the conditional
distribution to exclude undefined values of delay, and see [Section
5](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6703#section-5){.relref} of
\[[RFC6703](#RFC6703){.xref}\] for background on this analysis
choice.[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-2){.pilcrow}

See [Section
4.3.2](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.2){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\] for a closely related method for
calculating this statistic; see also [Section
4.3.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6049#section-4.3.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC6049](#RFC6049){.xref}\]. The formula is as
follows:[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-3){.pilcrow}

::: {#section-9.4.2.3-4 .alignLeft .art-text .artwork}
       Max = (FiniteDelay[j])

[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-4){.pilcrow}
:::

-   [such that for some index, j, where 1 \<= j \<= N
    FiniteDelay\[j\] >= FiniteDelay\[n\] for all
    n[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-5.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.4.2.3-5.1}

[]{.break}

Max:
:   The time value of the result is expressed in units of seconds, as a
    positive value of type decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see
    [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.000000001 seconds (1.0 ns), and with lossless conversion to/from
    the 64-bit NTP timestamp as per [Section
    6](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5905#section-6){.relref} of
    \[[RFC5905](#RFC5905){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.3-6.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::

::: {#section-9.4.2.4 .section}
##### [9.4.2.4.](#section-9.4.2.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Percent_LossRatio](#name-percent_lossratio-3){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-percent_lossratio-3}

For LossRatio, the count of lost packets to total packets sent is the
basis for the loss ratio calculation as per [Section
4.1](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7680#section-4.1){.relref} of
\[[RFC7680](#RFC7680){.xref}\].[¶](#section-9.4.2.4-1){.pilcrow}

[]{.break}

Percent_LossRatio:
:   The numeric value of the result is expressed in units of lost
    packets to total packets times 100%, as a positive value of type
    decimal64 with fraction digits = 9 (see [Section
    9.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc6020#section-9.3){.relref} of
    \[[RFC6020](#RFC6020){.xref}\]) with a resolution of
    0.0000000001.[¶](#section-9.4.2.4-2.2){.pilcrow}
:   
:::
:::

::: {#section-9.4.3 .section}
#### [9.4.3.](#section-9.4.3){.section-number .selfRef} [Metric Units](#name-metric-units-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-metric-units-6}

The \<statistic> of round-trip delay is expressed in seconds, where
\<statistic> is one of:[¶](#section-9.4.3-1){.pilcrow}

-   [Mean[¶](#section-9.4.3-2.1){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.4.3-2.1}
-   [Min[¶](#section-9.4.3-2.2){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.4.3-2.2}
-   [Max[¶](#section-9.4.3-2.3){.pilcrow}]{#section-9.4.3-2.3}

The round-trip loss ratio is expressed as a percentage of lost packets
to total packets sent.[¶](#section-9.4.3-3){.pilcrow}
:::

::: {#section-9.4.4 .section}
#### [9.4.4.](#section-9.4.4){.section-number .selfRef} [Calibration](#name-calibration-6){.section-name .selfRef} {#name-calibration-6}

[Section
3.7.3](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc7679#section-3.7.3){.relref} of
\[[RFC7679](#RFC7679){.xref}\] provides a means to quantify the
systematic and random errors of a time measurement. Calibration in-situ
could be enabled with an internal loopback at the Source host that
includes as much of the measurement system as possible, performs address
manipulation as needed, and provides some form of isolation (e.g.,
deterministic delay) to avoid send-receive interface contention. Some
portion of the random and systematic error can be characterized in this
way.[¶](#section-9.4.4-1){.pilcrow}

When a measurement controller requests a calibration measurement, the
loopback is applied and the result is output in the same format as a
normal measurement, with an additional indication that it is a
calibration result.[¶](#section-9.4.4-2){.pilcrow}

Both internal loopback calibration and clock synchronization can be used
to estimate the available accuracy of the Output Metric Units. For
example, repeated loopback delay measurements will reveal the portion of
the output result resolution that is the result of system noise and is
thus inaccurate.[¶](#section-9.4.4-3){.pilcrow}
:::
:::
